  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=7.5)
    The story demonstrates originality in its premise and execution. The writing avoids purple prose while maintaining literary quality. Character emotions are shown through physical reactions rather than stated feelings. Some phrases like "slaves to the lullaby of conformity" feel slightly overwrought. The narrative maintains consistent tone and style throughout. The ending avoids predictability with its revelation of the director's similar rebellion.

  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=7.6)
    While the story demonstrates considerable originality in its approach to a landlord-tenant interaction, certain metaphors ("like a canvas awaiting the first stroke") verge on familiar territory. The landlord's philosophical nature occasionally risks becoming too ethereal, though this is largely balanced by practical moments. The prose maintains consistent style and avoids purple tendencies, with emotional resonance emerging organically from the interaction rather than being explicitly stated.
